Current Affairs Commentary

Peace and Disarmament 32

—Shi

U.S. President Roosevelt has a positive outlook on the upcoming World Economic Conference. The United Kingdom and the United States have also reached an understanding. The future of the world economy seems to be opening up a new situation from the panic. However, political crises are lurking everywhere. The opportunity for war and turmoil is not only appearing in Europe but has also manifested itself in East Asia. Therefore, President Roosevelt wanted to take the initiative and first proposed a peace declaration, and supported British Prime Minister MacDonald's disarmament proposal to eliminate the deepening of the current political crisis, thereby laying the foundation for the world economy. His intention is sincere and his behavior is also excellent. However, we must have a proper understanding of the current world situation to avoid misrecognition of facts, especially political disputes, which should not be taken lightly. Otherwise, even if temporary peace is restored, it will eventually lead to unexpected events. This is what we hope President Roosevelt will pay attention to.

Since the beginning of March of this year, the Geneva Disarmament Conference has been almost paralyzed. After the British Prime Minister proposed a concrete disarmament plan, Germany insisted on "equality in armaments," France insisted on "security guarantees," and Japan vigorously implemented its military aggression, causing peace to fall into a stalemate. British Prime Minister's trip to Rome, the British-Italian understanding, seemed to be successful. The European dispute may have achieved a relatively understanding result. However, Germany and Italy considered it appropriate, while France believed it would harm its security, and Poland, the Czech Republic, Romania, and other countries each held different opinions. The road ahead is rugged, and there may still be many obstacles. Therefore, the coordination plan of the four major powers was shelved due to France's unhappiness, Germany's obstinacy, and the opposition of the Little Entente countries.

We are well aware that the focus of the disarmament issue lies in Europe, especially the conflict between France and Germany. Germany advocates the revival of the German nation and has repeatedly expressed its interest in the so-called "corridor" region. Therefore, the demand for "equality in armaments" has become one of the "national policies" of the National Socialist Party, and the Geneva Disarmament Conference has suffered even greater setbacks.

The U.S. President declared to uphold peace and hoped that all countries could accept the disarmament plan proposed by British Prime Minister MacDonald on March 16 of this year. We recall that more than two months ago, Germany insisted on dissatisfaction with the restrictions on land and air forces, and the plan came to a standstill. Hitler's threat caused the displeasure of the United Kingdom and France. What Germany gained was almost zero, and the world economy deteriorated further. Therefore, after the U.S. President proposed universal disarmament, Germany had to express its acceptance to show its moderate spirit and avoid falling into international isolation. Therefore, in the tense atmosphere of the European continent, a glimmer of hope for peace reappeared.

However, the situation in the Far East is very different. Japanese militarists still maintain their long-standing means of aggression. On the surface, they support the strengthening of the "Kellogg-Briand Pact" and greatly agree with the commitment of countries not to invade each other. However, they reserve the so-called "exercise of the right of self-defense." What's more, they even make the special circumstances of the Far East an exception, and the act of armed forces crossing national borders is the activity of the army as police. If this reservation is established, not only will world peace be completely destroyed, but international disarmament will also be empty talk. Moreover, in fact, although the European continent is shrouded in dark clouds, the state of peace has not yet been broken. As for the Far East, the Japanese have already launched military force and are now gradually carrying out aggression to achieve their ambition of gradual encroachment. In this case, it is difficult to desire disarmament and the success of peace.

Four-Power Pact Nearing Completion; Mussolini to Announce Today 33

Rome – Negotiations for the Four-Power Pact between Italy, France, Germany, and England have continued to progress this week. The visit to Rome by Göring, a key figure trusted by German Chancellor Hitler, can be seen as proof that the drafting of the pact, which has been underway for several weeks in the diplomatic sphere, is now nearing completion. The British Ambassador, Sir Ronald Graham, met with Italian Prime Minister Mussolini this morning, and it is widely expected that Mussolini will announce the completion of the pact in the Chamber of Deputies tomorrow. (Reuters, 21st)

(London) – Negotiations for the Four-Power Pact have made significant progress in recent days. According to official sources, diplomatic talks regarding the pact are being conducted continuously in London, Paris, Rome, and Berlin. These negotiations had been somewhat sidelined due to general public attention on the preliminary talks for the World Economic Conference, but the sudden arrival of Prussian Prime Minister Göring in Rome has once again drawn attention to the matter. According to a Reuters correspondent in Rome, Göring's visit has greatly enlivened diplomatic activity, and rumors suggest that after meeting with Göring, Italian Prime Minister Mussolini will meet with the British and French ambassadors. (Reuters, 20th)

(Berlin) – Following today's meeting between Italian Prime Minister Mussolini and the British and French ambassadors to Italy, a Berlin news agency announced, citing sources in Rome, that negotiations for the Four-Power Treaty appear to be on the verge of success. It also stated that, under these circumstances, Prussian Prime Minister Göring's presence in Rome is of exceptional significance. The news agency further reported, citing well-informed sources, that Germany will announce its support for the Four-Power Treaty within 24 hours. Once Germany approves, the treaty will be completed. (Havas, 20th)

Rome – Talks on the Four-Power Treaty continue. The draft proposed by Italian Prime Minister Mussolini appears to have entered its final stage. When meeting with Prussian Prime Minister Göring, Mussolini briefed him on his discussions with the British and French ambassadors. Göring departed for Berlin today. Italian officials are optimistic, stating that if a treaty is to be concluded between the four powers, it must be done before the opening of the London Economic Conference. It is widely believed that this expression of sincerity from the four powers will facilitate the success of the London Conference. Yesterday, Mussolini actively mediated on points of disagreement to bring them closer. This process appears to have made significant progress. It is reported that the draft treaty includes a preamble in addition to the main text. (Havas, 21st)

Rome – The Four-Power Pact initiated by Italian Prime Minister Mussolini, involving England, France, Germany, and Italy, has once again attracted attention due to the sudden arrival of Prussian Prime Minister Göring in Rome. Göring arrived here yesterday, initially said to be attending discussions on technical issues related to civil aviation. Göring has now met with Mussolini once or twice, and the content of their talks is highly confidential. Rumors suggest that this visit is related to the Four-Power Pact. Some circles in Rome believe that the key to the success or failure of the pact now lies in the hands of the Germans. (Reuters, 20th)

US Further Expresses Position After Publication of Roosevelt's Appeal 34

US Willing to Join Consultative Pact After Abolishing Offensive Weapons

Endorsing Economic Sanctions Against Aggressor Nations

(Washington) Tonight, the White House issued instructions to disarmament representative Norman Davis. The instructions, totaling eight pages, remain strictly confidential to avoid external commentary before the US attitude towards the British security plan is presented at the disarmament conference. These instructions were issued in response to Davis's request for a clear and detailed statement of US policy, as Europeans want to know what the US will do once the President's call for drastic arms reduction and the practical abolition of offensive weapons is assured. According to reliable sources, the US government is willing to participate in a consultative pact and even encourage other countries to adopt it, but only on the condition of genuine disarmament of existing armaments. However, those who frequently meet with the President and Secretary of State claim that the US will not join any pact without the abolition of offensive weapons. Discussions on disarmament have been ongoing for over a decade without effective results, and superficial measures will be futile. It is expected that Davis will declare in Geneva on Monday that if offensive weapons can be genuinely abolished, the US will endorse economic sanctions against aggressor nations. Secretary of State Hull declined to release the content of the instructions but indicated that after next Monday, the US position on disarmament and security will be clearly revealed, leaving no room for doubt. He also stated that Davis will not make any guarantees on behalf of the US until there is a genuine understanding among European countries. Currently, it is generally believed here that France will hesitate to relinquish its position in Europe granted by peace treaties without some pact guaranteeing military assistance and economic sanctions. To address France's concerns, the US government is now willing to conclude an agreement stipulating that all national armaments be subject to inspection by an international committee. (National Telegram, 20th)

Japanese Reply to US President's Telegram 35

Carefully Considering US Proposals

(Tokyo) The Foreign Ministry announced that the Emperor's reply to the US President's telegram is as follows: "I received your Excellency's telegram of the 17th of this month regarding the proposals of the United States government. I express my gratitude for your Excellency's message establishing world peace and eliminating economic stagnation, and I have instructed my government to carefully consider the matter." (Associated Press, 21st)

(Washington) According to well-informed sources, Japan, due to the situation in the Far East, intends to refuse to sign any disarmament convention that stipulates the abolition of "offensive weapons." The accuracy of these rumors has not been officially confirmed as of yet. (Havas, 20th)

Program of Events for World Economic Conference Announced 36

(London) The program of events for entertaining the delegates attending the World Economic Conference has been released. The conference will open on the afternoon of June 12, presided over by the British monarch. That evening, the British government will host a banquet for the delegates at Grosvenor House, with 600 guests. On the afternoon of the 17th, the British monarch will hold a tea party at Windsor Castle. On the 19th, the British government will host a banquet for representatives of the self-governing dominions, chaired by Dominion Affairs Secretary Thomas. On the evening of the 20th, the City of London will host a banquet for the delegates. Two days later, Lloyd's of London will hold a reception. On the evening of the 26th, the Lord Mayor will hold a grand banquet at the Guildhall. On the evening of the 28th, the Admiralty will hold a reception. On the 30th, the Speaker of the House of Commons, FitzRoy, will hold a reception. On July 1, Lord and Lady Astor will hold a garden party. In addition, there will be other special banquets. The British Cabinet committee preparing the British proposals has been meeting almost daily this week, chaired by Prime Minister MacDonald. (Reuters, 20th)

(London) Foreign Secretary Simon departed for Paris and Geneva from Heston Aerodrome at 11:40 this morning aboard a British military aircraft. (Havas, 21st)

(Paris) Foreign Minister Paul-Boncour departed for Geneva at 11:10 this morning. (Havas, 21st)

(Paris) It is believed here that Germany's unexpected acceptance of British Prime Minister MacDonald's disarmament plan is a tactic to force France into the difficult position of either accepting a plan without guaranteed security or bearing the responsibility for obstructing a solution. The future situation depends on what measures US representative Norman Davis will propose for security, what proposals German representative Nadolny will make, and whether the Four-Power diplomatic talks currently underway in Rome will yield results. French Foreign Minister Paul-Boncour met with the German ambassador this morning, and the French Cabinet will hold an important meeting tonight to draft instructions for Paul-Boncour, who is scheduled to depart for Geneva tomorrow. (Reuters, 20th)

Soviet Government Statement on Roosevelt's Appeal 37

Whether Japan Will Support Remains Doubtful

US Adopting More Active Foreign Policy Towards Far East

(Moscow) The Soviet government newspaper Izvestia today published an article on US President Roosevelt's disarmament appeal to the heads of state, stating that it does not fully represent the awareness of the more far-sighted elements within the United States regarding the current world situation. The newspaper said that the Soviet government's response will not use diplomatic ambiguities and evasions, as it considers President Roosevelt's proposal to be a step towards the policy that the Soviet Union has been striving to achieve since its founding. While Roosevelt only requests the reduction of armaments, he is sympathetic to MacDonald's disarmament plan. MacDonald's plan, on the one hand, represents a moderate approach to reducing offensive weapons, but on the other hand, it lacks universality and limits disarmament to Europe. The Soviet Union supports any proposal for partial disarmament, but it insists that disarmament must be universal, as it is a country based in both Europe and Asia. The Soviet government strongly agrees with Roosevelt's proposal that no country's troops should cross borders to invade another country. Roosevelt's call for the establishment of a universal non-aggression treaty is also consistent with Soviet policy. The Soviet Union's goal has always been to seek peace, so it will support any steps that facilitate this. If President Roosevelt wants to wage war against methods of economic aggression, he will meet with the Soviet government's firm support. The improvement of the lives of the various nationalities of the Soviet Union is increasing their demands, and the need for the Soviet Union to exchange goods with other countries is also increasing. The Soviet Union is a socialist country, but it enhances peace and eliminates obstacles to economic relations between countries, which is why it cannot support the policies of capitalist countries. It is doubtful whether President Roosevelt's appeal will be supported by the powers with whom he is in close diplomatic relations. His proposals will become a pawn in diplomacy, or be buried in the paperwork of capitalist diplomacy, or be drowned in a tide of insincere declarations. However, the Soviet government will sincerely support Roosevelt's proposals, as only the proletariat can support the rational proposals of the leaders of capitalist countries. Pravda also published an article on the matter, stating that the Soviet Union has always opposed the policy of aggression against other countries' lands and wealth, so President Roosevelt's proposal to conclude a universal non-aggression pact and oppose economic warfare will naturally receive the Soviet Union's support. It then discussed the contradictions between imperialist powers and the extraordinary economic crisis, and Roosevelt's declaration to preserve the results of the Geneva and London conferences to avoid tragic outcomes. The newspaper questioned whether the countries are willing to avoid such tragedies. The US President's appeal has only received lukewarm responses from the countries, with Japan openly opposing it and London rejecting it because it did not mention the war debt issue. The newspaper finally praised Roosevelt's declaration, saying that from a broad perspective, Roosevelt's appeal shows that, due to the world crisis and the situation in the Far East, the United States has adopted a more active foreign policy. The United States wants to find a way out of the current situation, and whether it can succeed will soon be seen. (TASS, 21st)

Central Committee Member Discusses Central Government's Foreign Policy 38

(Beijing) A Central Committee member told our reporter on the 21st: (1) The Central Government has always had a comprehensive and consistent foreign policy, particularly towards Japan, adhering to the principles of "no surrender" and "no compromise." However, due to national strength and various other factors, it is often in a passive position. Therefore, in addition to "no surrender" and "no compromise," it is necessary to assess the actual situation and adapt to circumstances. The recent intensification of the war demonstrates that the government will not be forced into submission by violent aggression. Huang Fu's trip to the north is purely due to the increasingly critical situation in North China and the unrest in Tianjin and Beijing. He is following the Central Government's instructions to reorganize the government and stabilize the public mind. Foreign policy is not his responsibility. Recent rumors that Huang Fu's trip north is to handle compromise, negotiations, troop withdrawal, and ceasefire are purely rumors, as far as I know. If the Japanese side wants to negotiate, negotiations can be held at any time. If we were to surrender, we would have already surrendered. Why wait until today, and why make such great sacrifices? As for the establishment of a buffer zone and the demarcation of Tianjin and Beijing as political areas, these are unilateral attempts by the Japanese side. Today, negotiations and peace depend entirely on the Japanese side. If they are sincere in negotiating, negotiations can begin immediately. If they want peace, peace can be achieved immediately. Our side only seeks to uphold the resolutions of the League of Nations and maintain territorial integrity. Any negotiations can be conducted on these terms. Otherwise, even if Tianjin and Beijing are lost and North China falls, it will be difficult to begin negotiations. (2) There are also many rumors regarding the current situation. Since the outbreak of the national crisis, the Central Government has been concentrating national strength and manpower to jointly seek solutions. At the same time, for the sake of consolidating the foundation of the country, it will never tolerate the Red bandits. Years of large-scale suppression have gradually been effective, but in order to completely eliminate them, special orders have been given to the Southwest to send troops to assist in the suppression, and senior officials have been appointed to be responsible for the campaign, so as to avoid the army resisting Japan from being constrained. In the Southwest, due to obstructions and delays, there is often a disconnect with the Central Government's administrative policies. The Central Government has repeatedly sent telegrams to explain, and they should be able to understand. However, outsiders do not understand the truth and believe the rumors, saying that the situation is about to change again. Regardless of the facts, I can say with certainty that in this time of national crisis, no one dares to risk being unjust. If someone disregards national interests and the safety of the nation, attempting to undermine the foundation of the country, it would be tantamount to digging their own grave and alienating themselves from the people. (3) The meaning of the Central Government's convening of a temporary national representative assembly has been reported in detail by President Wang at the Central Memorial Week. The Southwest initially inquired about the Central Government's intentions due to a lack of understanding, but after the Central Government sent telegrams to explain, they also understood. Rumors that the Southwest will convene a separate assembly in Guangdong are probably unreliable. However, any opinions can be contributed to the Central Government. The Central Government only seeks what is beneficial to the country and will adopt it without exception to gather ideas and broaden knowledge. If they listen to rumors and make reckless attacks, they will only cause disputes and be of no benefit. I hope that the people can work together with the government to overcome the national crisis. (Central News Agency, 21st)

US and UK Conducting Exchange Rate Stabilization 60

Roosevelt Invites Bank of England Advisor for Talks

Time Ripe for Stabilizing Gold-Dollar and Gold-Pound

(Washington) Today, US President Roosevelt suddenly invited Sir Otto Niemeyer, economic advisor to the Bank of England, to the White House for talks. Treasury Secretary Woodin was also present, and it is reported that consultations will continue tomorrow. It is widely believed that this is the first step by the US to stabilize international currency prices. The talks between Roosevelt and Niemeyer today were not announced beforehand, and stabilizing exchange rates has not been a major topic in recent talks between the US President and foreign representatives. However, US government officials indicated earlier this week that major financial countries will attempt to agree on a stable exchange rate agreement before the opening of the World Economic Conference, as there have been no drastic fluctuations in the exchange market recently, and the time is ripe for stabilizing the gold-dollar and gold-pound. As for silver prices, it is reported that they were not discussed today. Undersecretary of State Moley also stated in a radio broadcast today that the silver issue will be left to the London Conference to decide, and that it is now the time for central banks of various countries to maintain the closest cooperation. The fact that the silver issue must be left to the London Conference can be seen as an indication that the stabilization of the Anglo-American-French exchange rates will be the first priority. According to Moley, the main purpose of the silver issue is to sufficiently increase silver prices so as to increase the purchasing power of Latin America and China. As for the war debt issue, Moley only reiterated the US government's previous declaration, stating that it will discuss the issue individually with the debtor countries during the economic conference and that it cannot be discussed together with general economic issues. (National Telegram, 20th)

(Washington) News from Paris and London states that the US, UK, and France will establish a public fund to stabilize the prices of the franc, pound, and dollar. However, Secretary of State Hull stated that while representatives of major countries mentioned this issue to State Department officials during talks in Washington, no compromise was reached. (Havas, 20th)

(Washington) Professor Raymond Moley, Undersecretary of State and close advisor to President Roosevelt, published an article today warning the world not to have excessive expectations for the World Economic Conference and not to assume that the international monetary system can be restored immediately. It is also necessary to know that war debts cannot be exchanged for other things, and the world should not expect the economic conference itself to be able to devise a plan to solve various international economic problems and alleviate world suffering. Even with regard to trade barriers, it is difficult to launch a fierce attack on these barriers. The most difficult task of the economic conference is the removal of trade barriers. The silver issue is also important, not only as a problem of using silver as currency, but also as a problem of increasing silver prices so that countries in the East and South America can purchase American goods. He predicted that the economic conference may agree to immediately return to central bank implementation of monetary policy, supplemented by timely internal administrative expenses and the gradual removal of exchange restrictions. (Reuters, 21st)

The French-American War Debt Problem 61

(Washington) According to news from Paris, the French government firmly believes that the United States will not allow postponement of the war debt due on June 15th of this year. It has therefore decided that upon the expiration of the deadline, it will not pay any of the outstanding amounts, including those due on December 15th of last year. The White House is unwilling to comment on this news, and political circles are greatly shocked. It is said that Roosevelt has always believed that since war debts can be repaid with silver, the burden on debtor nations has obviously been reduced. All debtor nations should at least partially repay the war debt due on June 15th. Communication between Roosevelt and the debtor nations has been continuous. It is generally believed that when Roosevelt met with Sir Frederick Leith-Ross, financial advisor to the Bank of England, yesterday, they discussed this issue. What we should pay attention to is that although American political circles believe that there is no clear relationship between the war debt problem and the disarmament problem, they also recognize that they are intertwined. The attitude of the United States Congress towards the war debt will inevitably be affected by the outcome of the disarmament conference. Washington is very pessimistic about Geneva, fearing that the proposals to be put forward by the disarmament representative Davis in the name of the United States next week will not satisfy the expectations of Western countries. Faced with militaristic Germany, these countries may deem the United States' proposal insufficient and refuse to reduce their armaments significantly. However, from the perspective of the United States, Roosevelt's proposal, given the current attitude of Congress, can be said to have done everything possible. This can be seen from the declaration made by Democratic Senator Robinson in the Senate this afternoon. Moreover, even though the State Department has repeatedly urged the passage of the resolution authorizing the President to prohibit the export of munitions, the Senate has still shelved it and not voted on it. Under such circumstances, if Roosevelt makes people suspect that he is prepared to show generosity to debtor nations, his political position will be adversely affected. Therefore, Roosevelt is temporarily keeping silent on the war debt problem, waiting for the outcome of Davis's declaration in Geneva. If the European atmosphere clears up after Davis puts forward the United States' proposal, Roosevelt can then use it to advocate a policy of international cooperation with strong arguments. Conversely, if the disarmament conference fails, the failure of the London Economic Conference will be inevitable, and Roosevelt, under the pressure of public opinion, will inevitably turn around and issue another shocking declaration, saying that the United States will no longer be involved in European affairs. (Havas News Agency telegram, 20th)

Establishment of a Nude Club in Hong Kong 62

Siamese Overseas Chinese Inspection Delegation Visits the Capital's Construction 63

Delegation Members Discuss the Situation of Overseas Chinese in Siam

(Nanjing) Chen Wentian and others from the Siamese Overseas Chinese Return to China Inspection Delegation, along with Phirot Waiyachet, Secretary-General of the Siamese Ministry of Education, a group of six, returned to China from Siam last month. They inspected education construction and revolutionary sites in Hong Kong, Guangzhou, Shantou, Shanghai, and other places. They arrived in Nanjing from Shanghai a few days ago and are staying at the Overseas Chinese Guesthouse, where they are being guided and received by the Central Overseas Affairs Party Committee. They visited the Mausoleum of Dr. Sun Yat-sen and inspected National Central University, Jinling University, the Children's School for Martyrs' Descendants, Nanjing High School, Gulou Kindergarten, and other places. They repeatedly consulted with the Central Government, the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission, and the Ministry of Education regarding overseas Chinese affairs in Siam and how to resolve the problems of educational oppression by the Siamese government. They plan to stay in Nanjing for another two or three days before going to Shanghai and returning to Siam by ship. According to the delegation members, overseas Chinese in Siam often have limited understanding of the situation in their ancestral country. Since the revolution in Siam last year, new policies have been implemented, partly aimed at learning from China's culture and education, and partly aimed at assimilating the Chinese. Moreover, Japanese ambitions are very strong, and they are trying to take the place of the Chinese in Siam. In order to maintain Sino-Siamese relations and trade, transplant Chinese culture, and resist Japanese aggression, the inspection delegation was organized. The Siamese population is estimated at ten million, while the Chinese account for sixty to seventy percent. After hundreds of years of operation by the Chinese, the situation today has been achieved. The leader of the Siamese Nationalist Party is of Chinese descent, and most of the new policies are being managed by the Chinese. The Siamese people are afraid of the growing power of the Chinese, and coupled with the Japanese coveting, the overseas Chinese in Siam are truly worrying. The Siamese government has also restricted the Chinese in education and economics, and even restricted Chinese immigration, in order to establish a supportive policy for the new government. Under these circumstances, the overseas Chinese, even if they have become a force, will also decline. The Siamese government forces Chinese schools to teach Siamese for eighteen hours and forty minutes per week. If this continues, in a few decades, the Chinese will not be able to recognize Chinese characters at all, and will therefore become detached from their ancestral country. Therefore, they hope that the government will negotiate with Siam to abolish this rule. Otherwise, they hope that schools will be established in Shantou and Guangzhou, specializing in enrolling Siamese children of overseas Chinese, in order to break away from the constraints of compulsory education. In addition to invading our country, the Japanese also have a so-called southward policy, to compete with our overseas Chinese in Southeast Asia. They also collect art albums, supplemented with research, claiming that Japanese and Siamese cultures have been interconnected since ancient times and should be friendly to each other. They also take various Sino-Japanese treaties and print them in the Siamese Navy Gazette, to slander and insult and to alienate Sino-Siamese relations. If we do not urgently plan for this, the consequences will be unimaginable. (Central News Agency telegram, 21st)

Takahashi Dismisses Resignation Intentions, Saito Cabinet Achieves Minor Stability 79

▲ Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 21st: From the perspective of the current political situation, the retention of Finance Minister Takahashi by the House of Peers is a matter of course. Ultimately, Prime Minister Saito's success in retaining the Finance Minister can be seen as a victory for the pro-cabinet continuation faction. The House of Peers, feeling dissatisfied that the Finance Minister's resignation issue caused political unrest for a month and a half after the end of the parliament, advocated swiftly eliminating this unrest, publishing a political belief, and indicating the government's path forward. This is a major urgent task for Prime Minister Saito. On the government's side, because it is an emergency cabinet, it has been busy with various emergency countermeasures since its establishment. Now that it is entering its second phase of activity, the Finance Minister's resignation issue has repeatedly arisen, and the Seiyukai is trying to use this opportunity to sever ties with the government in order to gain a chance to overthrow the cabinet. The intention is clear, leading to a chaotic political situation. It is gratifying that the Finance Minister's clear political attitude was not calculated by the Seiyukai's conspiracy and he expressed his intention to stay. However, even if the Finance Minister stays, if the Seiyukai does not change its attitude of overthrowing the cabinet, the government will only achieve temporary minor stability, and the root of the disaster will still exist. Ultimately, the future of the political situation depends on the Seiyukai's attitude. Therefore, the Seiyukai will temporarily endure and wait for the development of the situation.

▲ Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 21st: Prime Minister Saito will meet with Finance Minister Takahashi tomorrow. Therefore, he returned to Tokyo from Hayama this morning at 9:00 AM with his wife.

▲ Japan United News Agency, Tokyo, 21st: After Prime Minister Saito visited Prince Saionji, the Seiyukai's long-held beliefs have been slightly shaken. However, there are currently two opinions within the party. One is the "advocate of separation" faction, who believe that the Finance Minister will never stay. However, if the Finance Minister's state of mind changes and he decides to stay, they believe that the mission of the current cabinet's establishment has been completed and advocate constitutionalism. When the government prepares the next year's budget, they will raise the Seiyukai's own policies and separate from the government, challenging the government with the determination to dissolve the parliament. The other faction is the "advocate of self-respect," who believe that the current cabinet is a so-called cabinet without direction or power, so the Seiyukai does not need to put pressure on it, and the government will naturally collapse.

▲ Japan United News Agency, Tokyo, 21st: Cabinet Secretary Horikiri visited Prime Minister Saito in Hayama last night around 8:00 PM, listened to the details of the meeting with Prince Saionji, and then left. The government believes that as a result of the Prime Minister's visit to Prince Saionji, the Finance Minister's retention can be expected to be realized, so it is optimistic about this issue. After meeting with the Finance Minister on the 22nd, the Prime Minister intends to ask the Finance Minister to publicly announce the reasons for his retention in order to stabilize the political situation.

▲ Dentsu News Agency, Hayama, 21st: On the way back from visiting Prince Saionji in Okitsu, Prime Minister Saito got off at Hayama to rest for the weekend. He told the press corps last night that the Emperor's reply to the US President's telegram was only to the extent of etiquette. The specific content must be studied by the government before a reply can be made. Regarding the Finance Minister Takahashi's resignation issue, Prince Saionji is aware of it and is not worried about the political situation. He very much wants to meet with the Finance Minister as soon as possible. The details of the conversation cannot be revealed until after the meeting. However, his hope that the Finance Minister will dismiss his resignation intentions remains unchanged, but he did not want to bother Prince Saionji with this. The government must first resolve the Finance Minister's problem and then address policy issues.

Paraguay Accepts the League of Nations Report 80

The Bolivian Representative Still Needs to Seek Instructions

▲ Reuters, Geneva, 20th: The Special Committee of the League of Nations handling the dispute between Paraguay and Bolivia discussed for more than three hours. The central issue is that regardless of the two countries' declaration of war, a state of war already existed before the declaration of war, and Article 15 of the League of Nations Covenant was not fulfilled. The Paraguayan representative immediately accepted the committee's report, but the Bolivian representative made a reservation and agreed to telegraph the matter to the government to request new instructions.

▲ National News Agency, Geneva, 20th: Today, the Council of the League of Nations held an emergency meeting. The Bolivian representative requested sanctions against Paraguay, saying that Paraguay declared war while mediation efforts were underway and four countries, Argentina, Brazil, Chile, and Peru, with the consent of Paraguay, were indeed plotting to achieve peace, which was a violation of the League of Nations Covenant. He also said that Bolivia had previously formally requested the invocation of Article 16 of the Covenant, but the report drafted by the Three-Member Committee of the Council of the League of Nations did not mention sanctions, which was deeply surprising. The report on the Paraguayan-Bolivian dispute drafted by the Three-Member Committee was then unanimously adopted, advocating an immediate ceasefire, the cancellation of the declaration of war by Paraguay, and the conclusion of an arbitration convention by both parties.

Germans Do Not Give Up on German-Austrian Unification 81

▲ Reuters, Berlin, 20th: Dr. Frank, Minister of Justice of the German state of Bavaria, recently went to Austria as a representative of the National Socialist Party but was expelled by Austria. Today, he gave a speech to students in Berlin, saying that we must not allow Austrians to be dragged into a situation that conflicts with German interests by a partisan government. We want to work towards German-Austrian unification, because this is a historical necessity and will be the ferry for the future unified Germanic nation. We cannot abandon this goal. The peace treaty clearly states the possibility of amending it through legal procedures, which is what we should strive to achieve.

▲ Havas News Agency, Vienna, 21st: Berlin students held a demonstration against Austria yesterday, presided over by Bavarian Minister of Justice Frank, and delivered a speech. Vienna newspapers have all expressed contempt and indignation at this demonstration. The newspapers are trying to avoid escalating the already tense situation, but clearly stated that Austria should seek autonomy and not be interfered with by foreign countries, even those of the same ethnicity. "The Federal Post" specifically refuted the National Socialist Party's slander of the Dollfuss government, saying that it had taken brutal actions, and protested Frank's declaration, saying that Austria had the freedom to take all measures. The communist "Red Flag" newspaper said that the new German ideology of Frank's mouth does not conceal that he intends to make Austria a sphere of German interests, to rank among Manchuria.

Huang Fu Arrives in Beiping, and the Beiping-Tianjin Security Issues 83

Stabilize the People's Hearts and Maintain Peace

Beiping Special Dispatch: After the Japanese troops penetrated deeper, Beiping and Tianjin felt threatened. All parties are striving for safety measures for Beiping and Tianjin. After Huang Fu arrived in Beiping, he has been continuously consulting with He Yingqin, Zhang Qun, Huang Shaoxiong, Jiang Bocheng, and important generals in Beiping, Shang Zhen, Xu Tingyao, etc., to earnestly coordinate. The first step is to stabilize the people's hearts and maintain law and order. Huang's visit to the north this time is all in accordance with the central government's intention, acting according to circumstances. The current method is neither compromise nor seeking peace, but to seek peace as the standard under mutual understanding. The initial step in seeking peace is to cease-fire. The armies on both sides must first stop the conflict, and then peace is possible. After the Japanese army advanced to a certain location, they did not advance further. Our army, since yesterday (18th), has also begun to retreat. On the Beining Line, our army is concentrated in Lutai, Ninghe, and other places, setting up defenses along the Duhe River. Tangshan is stationed with puppet troops, with two armored trains stationed in Xugezhuang. The vanguard is holding a position across the river between Xugezhuang and Tangfang with our army. Huang Fu still visited He Yingqin at Jurentang the night before last at 5:00 PM for a long discussion, exchanging views on diplomatic and military issues until late at night before Huang returned to Fengzeyuan. It is heard that they are still continuing to discuss the policy of stabilizing the people's hearts and consolidating law and order. After obtaining the central government's instructions, they will begin to proceed. How to proceed cannot be discussed at the moment. In the afternoon, Huang personally went to visit the Politician Tang Erhe at Beikoudai Hutong, Xisipailou. He had a brief discussion with Tang on diplomatic issues and returned to Fengzeyuan at 2:00 PM. Huang also sent Gao Lingbai to Tianjin to invite the Politicians Zhang Boling and Zhang Zhitang to Beiping. As for the Beiping-Tianjin circles, opinions are divided on whether to support or oppose the plan. Whether the future is smooth will depend on the development of the situation in the most recent days. (19th)

One Aspect of Japanese Military Conspiracy (Tokyo Dispatch) 84

Since Japan withdrew from the League of Nations, there have been two different viewpoints within the country on this matter. One is a radical theory, advocating active implementation of its continental policy in military affairs, rejecting the Soviet Union in the north, and invading China in the south. In diplomacy, they continue to be stubborn, supporting the so-called "scorched earth diplomacy," maintaining what they call isolation. Domestically, they vigorously promote a collaborative cabinet under the influence of the military clique, even if they don't outwardly deny parliamentary politics, they strive to explain the necessity of prolonging the state of emergency, and create emergency situations with military force. The other is a moderate and cautious theory, believing that militarily, this is enough, and they should maintain the peak of victory and not be rash, because encountering obstacles would not be worth it. Moreover, the atmosphere of international peace is also very strong, and it would be unwise for Japan to truly isolate itself.

The representatives of the former faction in the military are Army Minister Araki Sadao, Kwantung Army Commander Muto Nobuyoshi, Director-General of Education Hayashi Senjuro, and in literary circles, there are Uchida Kosai, and even Hirao Kiichiro. Among the latter faction, the more influential in the military are former Vice Chief of Staff Mazaki Jinzaburo, and the Governor-General of Korea, Ugaki Kazushige, supports him. In literary circles, there are some members of the Minseito (Constitutional Democratic Party). However, although the latter faction has the General Staff Headquarters in hand, the actual command power of the army administration and the troops in Manchuria is in the hands of the radical faction.

In fact, within the territory of the Three Eastern Provinces, the railway from Dunhua to the Tumen River bank has been completed, and the Japanese army's operations in the Northeast have become more convenient. So, it further developed its aggressive intentions. First, it increased the deployment of two divisions to Manchuria: the entire 7th Division of Asahikawa, the 16th Division of Kyoto, the 5th Division of Hiroshima, and the 3rd Division of Nagoya, drawing elites and sending them to the Northeast, transferring them west of Shanhaiguan, south of the Great Wall, to disturb Hebei, and also instructing Liu Guitang and others to harass Chahar from Dolon. At the same time, it used the excuse of detaining trains to oppress the Chinese Eastern Railway, and said that it would use force. Moreover, it often used the pretext of suppressing bandits to fire guns at the Soviet border, and even sent small units across the Soviet border. Of course, this was to test the true attitude of the Soviet Union. After several tests, it became clear that the Soviet Union was determined to continue its peaceful foreign policy. Therefore, it became more and more impolite towards the Chinese Eastern Railway, declaring that it would engage in border blockade. When the Soviet Union declared its willingness to peacefully transfer the Chinese Eastern Railway, it also stated that it was unwilling to buy it, and even if it did, the value must be below 80 million Japanese yen. This clearly shows that it wants to forcibly occupy it and is a symbol of intentional provocation.

However, people like Mazaki and Ugaki always felt that this was inappropriate, believing that being blindly tyrannical would easily lead to accidents. Little did they know that in fact, it was providing the radical faction with favorable explanations and a favorable environment. Therefore, the cautious theory was ultimately untenable. Mazaki Jinzaburo only got the empty title of General, and the two important military positions of "Vice Chief of Staff" and "Military Councilor" were squeezed out. Ueda Kenkichi (commander of the 9th Division of Kanazawa during the Shanghai Incident), whom the Araki faction trusted, succeeded Mazaki in order to implement his military expansion plan.

Originally, according to the ideals of the moderate faction, it was necessary to take international relations into consideration and not advocate invading Pingjin (Peiping and Tianjin). It should seize the opportunity to negotiate peace terms with China, and attack after the situation in Manchuria stabilized. The radicals believed that taking advantage of the fact that there were many international disputes and the world economic panic was still bottomless, they could do whatever they wanted, and they were not afraid of resistance from various countries. At the same time, they could not come forward to raise any objections. Therefore, he (the Japanese military) first made the three-in-one military giants丨丨General Staff Headquarters, Army Department, Director-General of Education Department丨丨 all the Araki radical faction, and cooperated with the Kwantung Army Headquarters in unison, which was convenient for dealing with China and the Soviet Union. Therefore, the peaceful and cautious theory is at most empty talk, and cannot affect any practical action. Therefore, the movement to overthrow the Saito Cabinet, from secretly brewing to open debate, but with the support of the military, has been extended to the present, and no one dares to launch it.

Their plan for North China is to use Tianjin as a base to buy off disgruntled military officers to instigate riots, and to advance their troops in the front lines from Luanzhou and Fengrun to Miyun to put pressure on Pingjin. At the same time, it threatens Shandong and Shanxi, dispersing the gathering power of the Chinese army, in order to implement its old strategy of defeating them one by one, and develop its ambition to invade North China. (May 16, 1933, Tokyo)

Japanese Planes Reconnoiter Beiping Three Times

Anti-Aircraft Shells Injure Civilians

A special dispatch from Beiping. Amidst the rumors of a shortened front line, Huang Fu has arrived in a flurry. He is currently planning measures to calm the people's hearts. The people of Beiping, who were in the midst of a stormy sea, were at a loss. Because of Huang's arrival in Beiping, they began to believe that the central government will have concrete solutions to national crisis, and they are all delighted.

In recent days, the various armies on our front lines have been concentrating on their designated positions. Since the 17th, the eastern front and the defense zone south of Shixia Town have all been in a state of armistice. The situation in North China seems to be developing in a new direction. It is said that each army will undergo some adjustments in the near future. The troops of Wan Fulin and He Zhuguo, which have withdrawn from the battlefield this time, are concentrating their troops in the Yangcun and Langfang areas to reorganize and learn from, and will take a short period of rest and recuperation. They will not be sent to the front for the time being. Although Japanese planes are very active on both sides of the western section of the Beining Railway, there are no active movements. However, nearby villages are often in danger of being bombed, and many villagers have fled to places such as Pingjin. Most of the farming has been suspended. The future food shortage is truly unimaginable. On the Beining front, most of the Japanese troops are gathered in the Kaiping area. Only a small part of the Japanese artillery and more than 2,000 troops of the puppet state army led by Li Jichun entered Tangshan. Our front line is near Xugezhuang, and most of the troops are guarding the Tangfang area. On the evening of the 17th, Japanese armored vehicles once drove to the east of Xugezhuang, lingered for a long time, and then returned to Tangshan Station. This morning (the 19th), two Japanese armored trains came from Tangshan again, stayed briefly in front of Xugezhuang, and then returned to their original route. Our army is deployed on the west bank of the Dou River, the atmosphere is quiet, and there is no battle. On the Pingyu Avenue, our army is still guarding near Yutian, and most of the troops are concentrated in the Gushudian and Lindong areas. After the Japanese army captured Fengrun, most of the troops did not actively advance. It is estimated that there are about 10,000 people stationed near Fengrun. Around 11 a.m. on the 17th, a part of the Japanese army entered Yutian, but only a little over a thousand people. The Japanese army, the Hattori Unit, which occupied Zunhua, has intentions of approaching Shimen Town. Our army is still firmly defending Jixian. The defense zone south of Shixia is still guarded by our army and there has been no change. Three Japanese planes flew to Jiusongling this morning to scout, and dropped bombs, but our army was in the trenches and suffered no losses. As for the Japanese army in eastern Chahar, they are still in Dolon City. Although Liu Guitang, Zhang HaiPeng and the puppet army are planning to attack Guyuan, they dare not act rashly because our army's defenses are tight. The voices of withdrawing troops from Pingjin are getting louder and louder, and the curtain of the current situation has gradually been lifted.

Japanese planes have not been to Beiping for days, and people's hearts have gradually become stable. Unexpectedly, at 9:15 a.m. this morning (the 19th), there was a buzzing sound in the sky again. A Japanese plane flew from the northeast, passed over the city, and flew to Nanyuan to scout. Before long, it returned, circling the entire city several times. Our soldiers guarding the city opened fire with machine guns and anti-aircraft artillery as usual, firing into the sky. The Japanese plane flew north, and came again more than half an hour later. Finally, it flew back to the northeast. It hovered over Beiping for more than an hour, and the atmosphere of relaxation suddenly became tense again. Residents in each city informed each other, and street gossip was all about the planes. The frightened situation was roughly the same as when Japanese planes first scouted Beiping. At that time, Huang Ronghai (also known as Huang Qishun), who sold soda at a stall on the side of the road in the east market entrance of Shuimo Hutong, Dongdan Archway, was near the Henglisheng Coal Shop. The eaves of the shop were hit by an anti-aircraft shell by mistake. With a crash, the roof tiles were smashed. Huang was unable to dodge in time and was hit in the right arm and leg, and was seriously injured. The police station in the first district sent a police officer to Xiehe Hospital for treatment, but his life was not in danger. At that time, a pedestrian named Liu Er and two rickshaw pullers were slightly injured and were not in serious condition. At No. 89 Zhouma City Street, Xuanwumen Outside, the Henan Fellow Association also found a shell. It flew from behind the west room of the association, and the roof tiles were lifted up by the shell. It fell directly outside the east room, penetrated into the room through the glass window, and smashed teapots, teacups and other objects. Resident Zhao Wenliang had already gone out, so he was fortunate not to be injured. In the empty field of the Second Court of the Law School inside Xuanwumen and on Shangxie Street, there were also the same shells falling, but there was no damage. Afterwards, reporters investigated from all parties and believed that the three times that Japanese planes flew over Beiping was a threatening action by the Japanese army, and its intention was still to confuse people. It is said that this morning there was also a Japanese bomber plane that flew to Niulanshan in Shunyi County, northeast of Beiping, and dropped several bombs. The losses are unknown. For a time, rumors spread again in Beiping, and there were various rumors. It is widely rumored that the Japanese army will take further threatening actions before the situation in North China can be stabilized. (19th)

Rioters Throw Bombs, Japanese Soldiers Provoke Security Forces

East Station Bombed and Damaged, Beining Railway Car Catches Fire

A special dispatch from Beiping. At 10:30 p.m. on the 19th, a bomb was thrown and exploded on Guangxing Street in the Japanese concession of the Chinese area of Tianjin by reactionary elements. At 11:30 p.m., another bomb exploded in the South City. At 11:40 p.m., more than 20 Japanese soldiers, fully armed, went to Nankai School to provoke our security forces, demanding to visit the school. Our security forces stopped them, saying, "It is late at night, and we cannot visit." The Japanese soldiers immediately fired a volley and threw four hand grenades, snatching four rifles from our side. Our security forces did not fight back and immediately reported to their superiors, who ordered them to remain calm and respond accordingly. At 12:00 a.m., the Japanese barracks in Haiguang Temple fired four cannons again. The gunshots were as dense as a string of pearls. Plainclothes teams were being assembled in Fushimi Street, ready to go. At 1:00 a.m. on the 20th, the artillery fire had not stopped. The plainclothes teams rushed out of the Japanese concession and occupied the 6th district of the 2nd district. The situation was quite serious.

Reactionary elements lurking in a certain concession originally planned a riot on the 18th night, and issued gun passwords, dividing into three routes to attack the Chinese territory. One route attacked the Provincial Government, the Public Security Bureau, and the First Army Headquarters. The second route attacked the East Station. The third route attacked the Caojia Garden Garrison. Their passwords were (1) "Launch", (2) "Love the People", (3) "Success". Temporarily, due to our strict defense, it did not launch. At 12:30 a.m. on the 19th night, our security forces captured two traitors at Nanmenkou, one named Liu Yuqi and the other named Zhang Chenglin, and seized pistols, symbols and other items. They were immediately taken to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation. Also, on the 19th night, the security in various Chinese concessions in Tianjin became more serious. The Japanese military headquarters in Tianjin ordered the resident corps to inform Japanese and Korean residents to seek safe areas to avoid danger. Merchants in the Japanese concession were also notified by the Japanese police station to close their doors at 8:00 p.m. All important intersections in the south city, the southeast corner of the city, and the Wanguo Bridge were inspected more strictly. All cars and trams must be inspected, especially in the first, second, and third districts, where martial law was declared from 9:00 p.m., prohibiting pedestrians. The French Engineering Bureau also sent patrol officers to inspect the borders between the French and Japanese concessions, and sent armored vehicles to shuttle back and forth. The righteous troops stationed in Tianjin were also fully mobilized to guard the Italian concession. On the 20th, the Tianjin Japanese military headquarters also released many military pigeons with various slogans hanging on their tails. The 10th military train on the Beining Road arrived at the East Station from Tanggu at 8:00 p.m. on the 19th. After the passengers had unloaded, just as the passengers going to Peiping had boarded the train, a soldier saw a wicker package on the first platform, unattended, and smoke was rising from it. He reported it to the railway police. After the railway police checked it, they knew it was bad and immediately left. Suddenly, there was a loud noise in the wicker package. The soldier was bombed, and his flesh and blood flew everywhere. The station was bombed, with an area of ​​four feet deep and six feet in diameter. All the glass in the station was shattered, and the glass in the houses within 100 meters outside the station was also shattered. The 10th train was bombed and caught fire, burning down one first-class special car, one second-class car, and two third-class cars. There was one remaining car. At that time, the fire was very large, and the fire brigade could not rescue it. The locomotive pulled each car to the water tower outside Yangqi, moving back and forth to spray water to extinguish the fire until 10:00 p.m. One railway police officer and more than a dozen passengers were injured, and there were others who had not been identified. At 10:40 p.m., another bomb exploded, the location is unknown. (20th)

A Glimpse of the Chaos in Sichuan 87

Tian Songyao Abandons Responsibility for Suppressing Bandits

Troops are Drawn to Aid the 28th Army

Chongqing Dispatch. Since the outbreak of the second Sichuan war on the 14th of this month, the 24th and 28th armies have been fighting fiercely for days, and the deaths on both sides are over a thousand. Tian Songyao's 29th Army, which is currently busy suppressing the Red Bandits in Tong, Nan, and Ba areas, has been affected by the war in the rear and has stopped its operations. A large part of the front line has been drawn to the rear, claiming armed mediation, but in fact, it is assisting the 28th Army to attack the 24th Army. As for Yang Sen's 20th Army, Luo Zezhou's 23rd Division, Li Jiayu's New Sixth Division in the northern route, and Liu Xiang's 21st Army in the east and south of Sichuan, they are all making military preparations to expand the scope. At the same time, the Red Bandits who are scurrying in the northwest of Sichuan have made a comeback and want to revive. Therefore, the entire Sichuan situation has fallen into chaos. Here are the details of the recent infighting of the Sichuan warlords.

(1) Deng Jinkang, the commander of the 28th Army, telegraphed all parties on the 18th, reporting the battle situation as follows: (omitted titles) According to the telegram from Huang Yin, the commander of our Second Division, the enemies facing us are the six units of Li Yushu, Peng Chengfu, Shi Zhaowu, Wang Yuanhu, Cheng Zimin, and Yu Songlin, linking up guns and cannons, and their strength is about 25 regiments. From the beginning of contact on the 13th, local battles occurred. Until dusk on the 14th, the enemy launched a general attack on our entire line. From Guanxian on the right to Qinggangshu on the left, the enemy's line was spread out within a hundred miles along the river, expanding the scope. The enemy facing Guanxian was fiercely attacked by our Gong Brigade, and many enemies were killed. He Mountain Society Collapses and Injures People 90

The Chenghuang Temple (Zhang Shicheng Temple) in Heshan, Fengqiao outside Changmen, has always held a race meeting every April. Since the revolutionary army settled down, it has not been held for several years. Unexpectedly, this year it will be held as usual. Yesterday (21st) was the date of the race meeting, and tens of thousands of men and women in the city and countryside went to watch. Although the Public Security Bureau prohibited it, it was ineffective. The ceremonial guards were extremely prosperous, and there were stilt walking and other things. However, due to the excessive number of people, the railing of the Jiangcun Bridge in front of Hanshan Temple collapsed, injuring a woman, but fortunately, there was no danger to her life. The cases of lost children and stolen items are countless and are strange social phenomena. Nantong

The Opening of Dasheng Yarn Factory 91

The strike at the Nantong Dasheng Yarn Factory has subsided. Li Shengbo, the manager of the factory, suddenly left Tong for Shanghai, causing problems with the resumption of work. All the workers of the factory telegraphed the Shanghai Dasheng Board of Directors, requesting them to urge Li to return to the factory to start the machines. On the 20th, directors Zhang Xiaoruo, Li Qiqing, Zhao Shuyong, and Wu Jicheng telegraphed back, "We have received your telegram. During this period of serious national crisis, our factory is heavily in debt and is affected by the decline in the market price of yarn, and is almost on the verge of being unsustainable. It is inevitable to reorganize and innovate. Unexpectedly, a strike occurred and has not been resolved so far. We are deeply worried about the danger of the factory. If it continues for a long time, it will inevitably lead to a loss of credit and there will be no way to resume operations. If the skin is not there, what will the hair be attached to? You must know that whether our factory can exist is not only related to the life of each worker, but also to local charity, education, commerce, security, and other aspects. If each worker can understand this meaning, they should eliminate the old habits and refresh themselves in the future, and abide by the factory rules in everything. If the work is in order, it will be possible to maintain credit and the source of funds will not be cut off. Our association can urge Manager Li to go to the factory as soon as possible to preside over the affairs as usual."

Various Cocoon Markets Open One After Another 92

The spring silkworm season is particularly good this year. Xiaoshan District is already harvesting cocoons, and Lin'an District has completely finished placing silkworms on frames. County Magistrate's Beating Leads to Death 93

Zheng Zhong, the head of the dispatch and receipt department of the county government in this county, was 26 years old and usually cautious and respectful. County Magistrate Wu Wentai recommended a fellow villager named Cheng Ji as his assistant. Cheng, who was over 40 years old, was extremely addicted to gambling, resulting in a deficit of more than 700 yuan of public funds. Recently, with the handover between the old and new county magistrates imminent, the matter was discovered. Cheng, under the pretext of borrowing money to make up for the deficit, secretly escaped without a trace. The county magistrate then placed Zheng under surveillance and forced his parents, wife, children, and other seven family members to move into the county government for custody, ordering them to pay Cheng's debt by the 19th. However, Zheng's entire family was detained, and there was no way to find Cheng. Therefore, no money was collected by the deadline. County Magistrate Wu Wentai was furious and went to slap Zheng three times, saying, "Choose between death or imprisonment." After being humiliated, Zheng was filled with resentment and swallowed more than two ounces of opium and died. After his death, blood flowed from his mouth and nose, and his family wailed endlessly. On the same day (19th), they drafted a complaint to the county government. The judge approved it, held a court session at night, and summoned witnesses. The plaintiff was Zheng's mother, Ms. So-and-so. The defendant, Wu Wentai, claimed illness and did not appear. The plaintiff requested the detention of the defendant. The judge said that he must wait for a telegram to the High Court for instructions. The defendant is currently the incumbent county magistrate of this county, and this official has no authority to detain him. He ordered them to withdraw temporarily and summoned them for another hearing.

Local News

Textile Experts Discuss the Decline of Chinese Yarn and Relief Methods 94

Seven Major Reasons for the Decline of Chinese Yarn

Two Fundamental Solutions

According to the Guowen News Agency, the National Federation of Chinese Cotton Mills previously unanimously decided to reduce working hours by 23% for a fixed period of one month due to poor sales. On the one hand, it appealed to the government to convene yarn merchants and the financial sector to discuss relief for Chinese yarn. There has been no thorough solution, and the one-month period of reduced working hours has expired. The future of Chinese yarn still faces many crises. Yesterday, a reporter met with a textile expert to discuss the crux of the decline of Chinese yarn and thorough reform methods. The following is a record of his detailed talk, which can also serve as a reference for the government and the yarn industry.

Overproduction Is Incorrect 95

The current decline of Chinese yarn, which has resulted in reduced working hours, is often attributed to overproduction by those who are unaware. However, this statement is contrary to the facts. The supply of cotton yarn in our country is still insufficient to meet the needs of the people. How can there be overproduction? Comparing it with the United Kingdom, the population of the United Kingdom is one-seventh of ours, while the textile industry in our country, calculated by the number of spindles nationwide, is only one-seventh of theirs. The number of spindles available for each person is only one-tenth of what is needed, therefore, our country's yarn industry needs more production, how can there be overproduction?

Reasons for the Decline of Chinese Yarn 96

However, although production is not excessive, the decline of Chinese yarn is indeed a fact. The reasons for this are extremely complex. Here are some of the reasons: (1) The financial sector concentrates money and refuses to circulate it, or the interest rate is too high to bear. The life of most yarn mills is in the hands of money lenders. This is one reason. (2) The Northeast has been occupied by Japan, and one-third of the Chinese yarn market has been seized. This is also a fatal blow. For example, the Nantong factories have 200,000 spindles, accounting for one-tenth of the national total, and their products rely entirely on the Northeast for sales. Since the occupation, the Northeast Chinese yarn market has been replaced by the Japanese. (3) The Shenxin Yarn Factory accounts for one-fifth of the cotton industry. In the past, it sold well in Yunnan and Guizhou. However, since the frequent internal turmoil, the exchange rate in Yunnan and Guizhou has fallen sharply. Seven Yunnan-Guizhou silver dollars are equivalent to one Shanghai silver dollar. Therefore, Shenxin cotton yarn has no possibility of being sold in Yunnan and Guizhou. This is a result of internal warfare. (4) The great floods in sixteen provinces last year and the civil war have weakened the purchasing power of the people. (5) In the Yangtze River basin, the Japanese sell low price goods at low prices. (6) The Japanese enjoy extraterritorial rights and can freely purchase materials in our interior to avoid taxation, while the Chinese yarn industry is subject to heavy taxes and miscellaneous levies when purchasing materials, resulting in high costs. (7) Compared with Japanese yarn factories, we only know that there is the Federation of Chinese Cotton Mills, but in fact, each operates independently and is not concerned with each other's problems. They are greedy for piecemeal transactions, and their products are of mixed grades and raw materials are not standardized. In addition, Chinese yarn factories, except for spinning coarse yarn that can use local materials, need to use American and Indian raw materials for the rest of the finer yarn. Wages are high, and expenses are large, but the products are not as good as Japanese yarn. On the other hand, the Japanese yarn industry adopts a trust policy, acts in unison in case of trouble, and manipulates the market. The raw materials they use are uniform, and the products are also uniform. As a result, their wages and expenses are more economical. In summary, the decline of Chinese yarn is based on these seven major reasons.

Fundamental Solutions 97

To revitalize Chinese yarn, there are two methods: (1) Our country has a population of 480 million, excluding producers, the remaining pure consumers account for about one-sixth, that is, 80 million people. All those within the reach of national government laws and regulations, such as the clothing and supplies of the army, civil servants, and young students, should be forced to use domestic products. With 80 million people supporting Chinese yarn, why worry about its decline? (2) Please ask the Chinese Yarn Federation to levy a tax of one tael on each piece of cotton yarn, which can yield 3 million yuan per year, and 15 million yuan after five years. Then use this fund to establish a cotton yarn bank, jointly run by merchants and officials, specifically to rescue Chinese yarn. If profits are made annually in this way, after ten years, not only can the Chinese yarn industry be as solid as a rock, but there will also be more than enough strength to eliminate foreign yarn.

Chinese Yarn Mills Decide to Continue Reducing Working Hours 98

Market Prices Slightly Improve, Costs Increase

Foreign Goods Dumped, Inventory Not Reduced

Chinese yarn mills, in accordance with the resolution of the National Federation of Chinese Cotton Mills, have implemented a 23% reduction in working hours since the 22nd of last month. After the day and night shifts were suspended for two days, Saturday and Sunday, today marks the end of the one-month period of reduced working hours. The Federation has resolved that after the expiration of the period, each yarn mill should decide on a plan based on its own situation. A reporter from Xinsheng News visited a spokesperson of the Federation. According to him, the Federation is not in a position to interfere with whether the factories will continue to reduce working hours after the expiration. However, at this time, when affected by the dumping of foreign goods, the yarn produced is bound to lose money, and the inventory of yarn has not decreased. The government has not yet implemented any relief measures. In order to maintain survival, it is feared that it will be difficult to recover.

Yarn Price Situation 99

As of the end of April, the total inventory of yarn in various factories in this city was approximately 160,000 bales. May ended yesterday. The lowest yarn price was 182 yuan per bale, and the highest was 192.5 yuan per bale. The lowest raw cotton price was 40.8 yuan per bale, and the highest was 46.95 yuan per bale. This week, the sales of Chinese yarn were mainly in South China, ranging from 1,500 to 2,500 bales per day. Last week, the sales of Chinese yarn were only from 200 to 300 bales per day. Although sales have increased and market prices have slightly improved, raw material prices have also increased accordingly. The yarn produced is still bound to lose money.

Continued Reduction of Working Hours 100

There are a total of 28 Chinese yarn mills in this city, including Hengfeng, Shenxin, Yong'an, Puyi, Weitong, Tongyi, etc., with approximately 1,117,000 spindles and approximately 7,800 looms. The accumulated yarn and cloth have not decreased. At this time of tight finances and high interest rates, it is really powerless to restore the original state. The factories have separately convened meetings and decided to continue the reduction of working hours, still reducing by 23%, and suspending day and night shifts on Saturdays and Sundays. Once the inventory of yarn is reduced and the market price improves, efforts will be made to restore as much as possible. However, Chongxin Textile Company in Tanjia Ferry maintains the original state because it did not reduce working hours last time. Jingwei Pengji Textile Factory on Yuezhou Road, being a waste cotton factory, also did not reduce working hours.

Implementing Austerity 101

In order to maintain survival, the Chinese yarn mills are implementing austerity measures while reducing working hours to save expenses. For example, Shenxin's sixth and fifth factories are laying off workers in various departments. Shenxin's first factory has canceled worker bonuses, which has aroused worker opposition. They have filed petitions with the Municipal Party Department and the Social Affairs Bureau for assistance. Party and government agencies have sent personnel to investigate the matter in order to mediate. It is heard that a few yarn mills, finding it still difficult to maintain operations after reducing working hours, plan to stop the night shift in the loom room and switch to the regular day shift. Those who used to work two looms per person are now working one loom, and the remaining loom is worked by a night shift worker.

Ministry of Industry Relief 102

According to the Central News Agency, regarding the issue of rescuing Chinese yarn mills, the central government has decided to borrow 20 million yuan from the financial sector in this city to provide relief. Minister of Industry Chen Gongbo, after arriving in Shanghai this time, has consulted with the financial sector and relevant parties in this city on the measures. According to banking sources yesterday, the banking sector can express its agreement on borrowing money to rescue Chinese yarn mills. However, the amount of the loan and the fund, etc., still need to be discussed. It is expected that after several more meetings, it can be determined. It is also learned that Minister Chen believes that the fundamental solution for Chinese yarn mills cannot be solved by borrowing money for relief. He plans to establish a Chinese yarn market in Shanghai to allow Chinese yarn to be sold throughout the country. Therefore, he has consulted with yarn merchants on everything and has achieved results.

Executive Yuan Proposes to Issue 2 Million Silk Public Bonds 103

Interest Paid by the Ministry of Finance, Principal Repaid by the Two Provincial Governments

In order to rescue the silk industry in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, the Executive Yuan has decided to issue the 2 million silk industry public bonds that were sealed and not issued in the 20th year (of the Republic). The interest will be paid by the Ministry of Finance, and the principal will be repaid by the governments of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces separately. Yesterday, the Ministry of Finance and the governments of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces were ordered to comply with this decision, and the Ministries of Industry and Finance were ordered to properly plan fundamental measures to enable the silk industry to revitalize itself. The original order is recorded as follows:

Order to the Ministry of Industry and the Ministry of Finance 104

For the purpose of issuing an order, it is found that the central government has issued silk industry public bonds twice in the 20th and 21st years to rescue the silk industry in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, but the silk industry is still declining. If this continues, it will not be able to reverse its decline, nor will it be within the reach of the central government's financial resources. In the future, proper fundamental measures should be planned to enable it to revitalize itself. The Ministries of Industry and Finance, together with the governments of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, should discuss and report on this matter. In addition to issuing this order separately, it is hereby ordered to comply with this.

Order to the Ministry of Finance and the Two Provincial Governments 105

For the purpose of issuing an order, the silk industry in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces has been declining recently, and various parties have repeatedly called for assistance. Relief should be given as appropriate. However, since the silk industry public bonds were issued twice in the 20th and 21st years, and with the country facing national disasters, the central government's finances are extremely difficult. In order to expedite matters, it has been decided to issue the 2 million silk industry public bonds that were sealed and not issued in the 20th year. The interest will be paid by the Ministry of Finance, and the principal will be repaid by the governments of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces. Each department (provincial government) should promptly plan and strictly comply with this, in order to comfort the longing of farmers and merchants. In addition to issuing this order separately, it is hereby urgently ordered to the department (provincial government) to properly plan the specific measures for paying interest (repaying principal) and report them for verification.
