Securities: Peace Sentiment Boosts Bond Market Last Week 214

A Sense of "The End of the Road and a Glimmer of Hope"

During the week of May 15th to 20th, the Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange's bond market experienced significant turbulence, with rapid price fluctuations. In an extremely adverse environment, a glimmer of hope suddenly appeared, creating a sense of "the end of the road and a glimmer of hope." Huang Fu's trip to Beiping and the US President's advocacy for peace acted like a stimulant for a weak body, instantly making it feel refreshed and full of energy. Market sentiment was uniformly excited, with the bond market expected to soar. Furthermore, with the May futures trading entering its final week, it triggered a severe short squeeze. Although large institutions and financial circles engaged in massive selling, it was like trying to stop boiling water with a ladle, proving futile and demonstrating the strength of market sentiment. However, in reality, it did increase a significant amount of capital, enough to ease the atmosphere considerably. On Monday, Beiping and Tianjin were extremely tense, with Luanxi, Tangshan, and Miyun falling one after another, and market prices continued to fall by several points. On Tuesday, news of Huang Fu's entry into Beiping emerged, and the atmosphere of peace became prevalent, causing market prices to rebound sharply. Various groups bought in, creating a surge. The price rose by 1.67 yuan throughout the day, causing short sellers to panic even more. On Wednesday, they continued to cover, and the price continued to rise by about half a yuan. On Thursday, the situation became even more tense with the US President's peace appeal, and the price rose even more sharply. However, this prompted large institutions, "No. 32," and financial circles, "No. 46," to sell massive amounts of salt revenue bonds, causing the salt revenue bonds to plummet by 1.2 yuan at the close. The previous gains were offset by the later losses, creating a contrasting and colorful picture. On Friday, "No. 66" continued to sell, but short covering surged even more, and market prices continued to rise by 89 points. On Saturday, due to riots in Beiping and Tianjin and the lack of factual evidence of peace, market prices weakened slightly by about half a yuan. As a result of the week, the total increase ranged from several points to over two yuan. Summarizing the trends of the past few days, the peace sentiment coincided with the approach of settlement, triggering a fierce short squeeze. As market prices rose, it also triggered the sale of physical goods by financial circles. The floating shorts all found a way out as a result. The trend from now on will certainly continue to fluctuate significantly. If peace is achieved, prices will continue to rise. If peace remains an illusion, then Beiping and Tianjin will inevitably be devastated, and the bond price collapse will be even worse than before the short squeeze. This is because a batch of floating longs will inevitably be added after the short squeeze. Trading was brisk, and the number of transactions was very impressive, totaling 82.2402 million yuan. Among them, spot transactions accounted for 85,200 yuan, with salt revenue bonds accounting for the most among futures, totaling 22.735 million yuan. Demobilization accounted for 3.165 million yuan, consolidated tax accounted for 12.46 million yuan, the 1919 Customs Bonds accounted for 12.135 million yuan, and the 20-year and 20-Customs Bonds together accounted for 16.795 million yuan. Disbandment also saw 3.07 million, and the remainder ranged from tens of thousands to four or five hundred thousand. Most of the transactions were for forward dates. A total of 210 shares were traded in the Exchange.

Silk and Tea Suffer from Silkworm Disease Due to Sultry Heat and Sudden Cold 216

(Jiangdu) This year, both farmers and silkworms are struggling due to a lack of resources to raise silkworms. Most are borrowing money to buy silkworm eggs. Hatching is not going well. Areas with relatively large-scale silkworm rearing include Yiling City, En Yu Zhou, Liu Er Wei, and Hongqiao. When the eggs were received, the weather was sunny and warm, and the silkworm larvae developed smoothly. The early batches have already completed their third molt and are consuming leaves, with some already emerging from their fourth molt. The late batches have also completed their third molt and are consuming leaves. However, over the past week, the weather has been constantly changing, with continuous thunderstorms and hail, followed by sultry heat and sudden cold. This has caused the early silkworms to stop eating and lose their molts, while the late silkworms have developed black spots on their bodies and die within 24 hours of moving to the mat. Silkworm farmers are panicking. They are currently trying to remove the diseased silkworms and using heat to maintain the temperature in an attempt to salvage the situation.

(Shaoxing) It is also an improved silkworm farming area in Zhejiang Province. This year, farmers have found it difficult to increase the scale of rearing due to economic reasons. After hatching, the climate has been warm and suitable, and instructors have been assisting with guidance. The silkworm larvae have been developing well. The early batches in areas such as Tianle Township and Lizhu have already reached their fourth molt, while the late silkworms in areas such as Huajia Dian in Anren Township have also completed their third molt and are consuming leaves. However, in recent days, continuous thunderstorms and alternating cold and heat have caused changes in the silkworm larvae, leading to diarrhea, vomiting of black fluid, swollen heads, and delayed feeding, with many being discarded. With the silkworms about to spin their cocoons, this sudden change has caused silkworm farmers to feel extremely frustrated.

Sales of artificial silk in Shanghai are not improving, and stocks remain high, while the supply is becoming increasingly scarce. Only 94 boxes of British and French artificial silk were shipped in by French mail last week, still stored in the Shanghai Customs warehouse.

Informal Discussion

The Secret of Getting Rich 221

—

Recently, many miracles can often be found in newspapers. In addition to a certain comrade learning diligently under Mussolini after ceding national territory, they have also learned a little secret of getting rich. Since the secret concerns getting rich, it is of course most needed at present, even though those above are determined to destroy the country, and the common people have no wealth to protect. If we are lucky enough to have our fortune and luck written in the stars, we can get rich once in a big way. Then, at least we can order a large Ford aircraft from abroad. In case "luring the enemy deep" leads us all the way to Yuhuatai, we can simply ride the auspicious clouds and leave together.

So, what is the secret of getting rich? It is: the only way is to buy lottery tickets. Facts speak louder than words. It is said that more than twenty workers jointly won the first prize of 50,000 yuan. As a result, some decided to remarry instead of staying widowers, some decided to no longer be insignificant clerks in foreign firms, and some who suffered losses in the Shanghai war were able to prosper again. In short, sudden wealth can completely solve any major problem, and even buying a small official position and taking office immediately is not impossible. Of course, this is greatly related to luck, but the secret of getting rich lies in this.

Moreover, in the current period of national crisis, there are even more opportunities to use this secret. That is to say, there are currently so many types of lottery tickets, just like the "numerous and too many to list" in summer discount stores. However, the most reliable is something called ×××× Construction Lottery Tickets. The first prize is 500,000 yuan, and the second prize can also be 100,000 yuan each. In addition, it is declared in advance that there will be "full payment" without any deductions. Therefore, this type of lottery ticket is not only very hopeful (because "one out of every ten tickets will win a prize"), but also very reliable. Not only that, but in addition to "huge prize amounts" and "rare opportunities," there is also the upright political significance of "both helping construction" and "receiving bonuses."

Regarding this section, it is indeed very exciting. In fact, apart from saving the country through aviation, there is no other way. Moreover, striving for construction amid national panic is even more of an astonishing move to make the enemy gasp. However, great construction requires huge amounts of money, and huge amounts of money can only come from the broad masses. Thus, there is this unique and wonderful method of "the whole country benefits, and everyone can win prizes," allowing us common people to "quickly join the work for the country and the family" after buying a well-winged copper badge. No problem, just taking out ten yuan is considered fulfilling the responsibility of loving the country. If you can win a prize, of course, you will get both fame and fortune. So, in the end, I want to respectfully tell everyone, come on, "quickly join the work for the country and the family"!

The Sin of the Common People 222

— Huan Yi

Some things in the world are truly inexplicable. For example, the wealthy bosses who often possess hundreds of thousands of dollars in assets, are trying to have a son. Even though they have married dozens of concubines, they still face the sorrow of having no heir, because the inheritance problem is difficult to solve, leaving them at a dead end. At the same time, the coolies who live in grass shacks cannot even afford to eat, but their families are thriving. They see their children popping out one after another, and they can't afford to abandon them or raise them, leaving them at a dead end. In the darkness, the creator seems to be deliberately playing jokes on them.

Since the September 18th Incident in Shenyang, we unfortunately encountered the young marshal Zhang, the great inventor of non-resistance, who generously gave whatever they wanted, and successively handed over the three northeastern provinces, inviting the enemy into the customs in a mighty way. It is said that on the night of the September 18th Incident, when the sounds of gunfire erupted in Shenyang, he was dancing and singing with extreme joy. Later, Jinzhou was generously gifted, and Yuguan and Rehe also changed color. The situation in Beiping and Tianjin suddenly became urgent, threatening his dancing and golfing pleasures. He simply rolled up his bedding, loaded his years of hard-earned money—no, it was the fat of the common people—onto dozens of tarpaulin-covered trucks, transported it to the Shanghai concessions, settled down, and happily ran off to enjoy his blessings abroad.

In fact, in our vast Republic of China, there are wise, resourceful, brave, and skilled armed comrades who are said to be loyal and patriotic everywhere. Is it not the case when they fight among themselves? What declarations and telegrams, full of grand principles of serving the country and the people, are spoken with the eloquence of heaven. The young marshal Zhang, who is now striking and traveling, also used to flaunt his power and invincibility, making a heroic display more than once. But precisely when he converted to Zen Buddhism, (a certain celebrity initiated a Vajra Dojo last year, and our young marshal was also one of the initiators) and strictly forbade killing, he encountered this unfortunate event. The incense burner chased away the monk. Isn't it destiny?

"Duolun Fell" and "Tangshan Lost" were printed in large fonts in the most prominent positions in the newspapers. But in another corner of the newspaper, Sichuan's Army Commander Liu and Chief Commander Deng were heating up again, staging a repeat of last year's antics, and the atmosphere was extremely tense, with war clouds looming, and the situation had the potential to expand and affect the entire Sichuan. According to their telegrams, both sides were ultimately acting for the country and the people, and were forced to wage this just war. As for which country and which people they were fighting for, the telegram did not specify. Some people say: if they want to resist Japan, then at least they should wait until the enemy is right in front of them before resisting, so as not to fail the meaning of the word "resist." Especially in the art of war, familiarity is key. Taking advantage of this free time, it would be wise to practice among themselves first as a precautionary measure. When the enemy reaches Sichuan from the north bank of the Yellow River to the south bank of the Yellow River, and from the lower reaches of the Yangtze River to the upper reaches of the Yangtze River, the generals can rest easy and order the soldiers, who have experienced hundreds of battles, to prepare for a long-term resistance, with one soldier capable of holding off ten thousand. Wouldn't victory be guaranteed?

But, in short, in the final analysis, it is still the "deep sins" of our common people. Otherwise, why would we need to bother these warlord lords with their far-sighted plans! If they continue to protect us like this, I'm afraid that even the small place where the common people can stand will be gone!

Literature & Art

Sentiments 223

— Tang Daowu

What have I been doing with my pen all these years?

Silently waiting for advancement, deceiving myself.

My heroic spirit fades away in books and ledgers,

My grand aspirations are futile as time passes.

I often crave sleep to find my dreams of home,

And write poems to express my idle sorrows.

Unaccustomed to wandering, yet a visitor I remain,

Who knows the feelings in my heart?

Jia Yi's worries and indignation were in vain,

He could not wield the sun-retrieving lance to save the country.

The strategy was decided only after the enemy entered the critical pass,

Half the country was lost, yet they speak of peace.

Though the barbarians are said to be truly rampant,

Who caused the protective barrier to be lost in an instant?

From ancient times, hesitation has led to downfall,

Planning the defense, I sigh and delay again.

Middle Class Families 224

— Ai Hua

Although Mr. Wang is poor, his background is truly not humble. His grandfather was a Daotai in the Qing Dynasty, and his father also served as a magistrate. He even has an uncle who is currently working as some kind of bureau chief. Unfortunately, his ancestors didn't leave much property for their descendants, and his father died too early. By the time his mother raised him and his three siblings, almost half of their meager inheritance had been used up. After his mother died, the siblings divided the property, and what each person received was truly insignificant. He himself had already started a family. He has a wife, two sons, and a daughter. Because he only has a middle school education and lacks the ability to scheme, he can only teach some courses at a small school, earning forty or fifty dollars in salary. Including some interest from his property, his total monthly income is only sixty or seventy dollars. But how does he spend it? Although he is not a middle-class family, he can't be considered anything less than a middle-class person. The face of a middle-class person must be maintained. He can't live in a pigeon coop. At the very least, he rents two rooms on the upper floor, which costs thirty dollars in rent. His children, who are of school age, have to be sent to school. At the beginning of the semester, he has to prepare forty or fifty dollars for tuition and miscellaneous fees. His youngest son is still breastfeeding. He can't bear to let his wife hold the child and go out to buy things. Moreover, he comes from a prominent family, and he is not used to doing such things. So, he has to hire an old nanny, whose wages and food take up one-sixth or one-seventh of his income. When relatives and friends have weddings, funerals, or birthdays, and send invitations, he has to attend out of courtesy. When giving gifts, he certainly can't give small change. For closer relatives, he has to give at least three or four dollars. Although he can try his best to economize on food, he has to pay attention to the health of his family. In Shanghai, under capitalism, getting sick is even more terrible. Wasn't his second son suffering from illness due to malnutrition, and because he didn't have much money to see a doctor, he just died like that? So, he really puts in a lot of effort to maintain the face of this middle-class family. The formerly chubby Mr. Wang, with a face full of spring breeze, has now become the gaunt, dark-faced Mr. Wang. When you talk to him, he is always full of complaints, as if he has nowhere to vent. He often sighs and says, "A family like mine is truly in an awkward situation. I really don't know how to maintain it."

Correspondence from Shop Assistants

Brotherly Disputes 226

Editor:

There are two brothers, A and B, who are fellow countrymen. When dividing the property, there was still an unmarried younger sister. Therefore, they set aside two acres of land as the sister's future marriage expenses and all other costs. At that time, because A was not good at production, the relatives designated B as the custodian, stating that B would be fully responsible for taking care of the sister in the future. When the sister got married, all expenses were still shared equally by A and B: B never made any compensation. Now, more than twenty years have passed, and all the evidence of both parties has been lost, and the witnesses have also passed away one after another. Currently, A intends "Since all expenses have been shared equally, this land should be enjoyed equally. Since B has received more than twenty years of rent, A should also have the same right to take turns." But B only agrees to refund A thirty dollars, regardless of whether it's a gain or a loss, and settle it in one go. According to the current market price, this land is worth two hundred and thirty dollars. Therefore, A firmly disagrees; the two parties have reached a deadlock. If it's not handled well, they may even go to court; sir, what is your opinion on this matter? I respectfully request

Yours truly, Yao Muyuan

× × × ×

Editor's Note: Law is something that arises after society has no other way. Therefore, no matter what happens, if there is another possible solution, it is best not to consult it. Between brothers, what is valued is deep affection, so they should not resort to law. In this matter, A may fail in law. He can't produce evidence, and he can't find witnesses. Since there was an agreement beforehand, why did you take out money when the sister got married? Unless you were willing to donate it, you should have obtained B's written statement. How can donated items be claimed from a third party? Moreover, since B has openly occupied these two acres of land for more than twenty years, and A has never raised any objections, the law has no way to recover it for you. However, in terms of human relationships, B really has an obligation to consider compensating A. As we see it, A's situation must have been worse than B's at first; when the sister got married, A's situation must have been better than B's: and now A is probably not as good as B again. So, even without this entanglement, B would have to take care of A to some extent, especially since he still has some reasons! This matter depends entirely on the intermediary to persuade him properly; to make A understand that he may not win in law and make concessions; and to make B reflect on himself, consider the facts, and give more.

Fiction

The Life of the Five Sisters (14) (Book) 227

— Ling He

13, Poor Child

This afternoon, the young master Zhang was indeed sitting in Miss Liu's living room.

Miss Liu came down from upstairs, the heels of her leather shoes making a slight low sound on the carpeted stairs. As usual, she had a tired heart, but her face was filled with a dignified and beautiful smile. Although she herself felt that this kind of smiling face was somewhat unnatural, it was also a kind of profound art. This art was something she had gained arduously in the course of her life. Just from this point, it can be seen how clever our Miss Liu is.

When she walked into the living room, the first thing she saw was young master Zhang bowing to her in a very polite and large angle. After that, his eyes were shining with excitement, and if you looked carefully, it seemed that even the muscles on his face were trembling slightly. However, this graceful and elegant behavior made Miss Liu feel amused, although at the same time it also gave him a little bit of goodwill of pity in her heart.

"I'm being very presumptuous, Miss! Can you not hate me for coming to visit you so boldly?"

"No, Zhang... um... what should I call you? Haha..." She covered her laughter with her handkerchief.

"As long as you're happy, Miss! Isn't it okay to call me anything? My name is Wenbin."

"Then I'll just call you Mr. in a very ordinary way. Do you like this title? Maybe it's too plain."

"No, Miss! This is already very good."

"I guess this is your first time coming to my house, right? It seems like we've never met before."

"That's right, today is my first time coming to your residence. But I've seen you before, it was the night before yesterday when Minister Su, Mr. Su Gengyun's mother had her birthday. It just so happened that Minister Su insisted on me helping with the reception, and we met that night. But because there were too many guests, and I'm not good at entertaining, you probably don't remember much."

"Ah! So that's how it is, then does that mean you and Minister Su are also relatives?"

So young master Zhang took the opportunity to explain; he is now a first-class clerk in the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and Minister Su is his direct superior. He spoke in fluent Mandarin. This made Miss Liu very enthusiastic, and between his eyebrows and dancing, there was indeed a lot of youthful and handsome air. As for his every move, he was also very dashing, even to the point of striking a match, it was also very romantic and not vulgar.

This time she talked to him enthusiastically for a long time, until she lazily leaned back on the sofa and yawned. Finally, listening to him very sincerely asking her:

"Tonight, can I accompany Miss to the theater once?"

"But she didn't agree, saying that she wasn't feeling well, and also advising him not to spend money on her. Afterwards, he said in a pleading tone:

"Then will you allow me to visit you again sometime?"

"You wait, I'll personally call you to invite you." After saying that, she added a touch of rich smile. But it could be seen that he was still very uneasy, so when she sent him to the door, she said more gently:

"Thank you for your kindness, let's meet again."

She watched his back, waiting until she uttered a sentence at her lips:

Film Supplement

Three Weeks of Hellish Work (Part 1) 228

— Yi Fan

A Glimpse into the Difficult Life of Actors

Jean Hersholt Recalls Events of Ten Years Ago

Robert Montgomery recently went to Hawaii to film "Hell Below." After returning, he talked to people about the various difficult tasks of filming near the volcano. An old actor named Jean Hersholt heard this. He said, "This is nothing. When I was filming 'Greed' in Death Valley ten years ago, that was scary." People then asked him to talk about the story of ten years ago. It was indeed very terrifying. Now I will translate it, which can show the general Chinese actors what kind of sacrifices they should be prepared to make for the sake of realism when foreign productions are made, and how much perseverance they should have, so that their lives are in danger or even lost. The following are the words of Jean Hersholt:

Death Valley ten years ago was very different from what it is now. Now there are places to avoid the heat, and there are roads leading to it, but in 1923, it was still like 1848, when the Bennett Expedition was trapped in thousands of miles of white sand and died of thirst. Because there is not a drop of water in Death Valley, and not a blade of grass grows, the temperature is as high as 160 degrees. In the summer, even the native Indians dare not set foot on it. But I and the other actors, under the guidance of director Erich von Stroheim, actually set off for Death Valley in July, the hottest month of the year.

After we passed through Long Pine and filmed a few scenes, we arrived at Skidoo, a small village outside Death Valley. The radio on the car suddenly broke down. So, from that point on, we were cut off from the civilized world. Later, we moved forward to Darwin, where I encountered another very unfortunate event. Because the horse I was riding was an uncontrollable bad horse. He threw me off and I was seriously injured. But there were no doctors in Darwin, so someone had to be sent to Bishop to ask for a doctor. I had to endure the pain and wait quietly for the doctor to arrive. Later, the doctor came and, after an X-ray examination, knew that I had broken two ribs and injured my hip bone, and I would have to rest for at least three weeks before I could work.

Director Erich von Stroheim had no choice but to leave me behind and set off on his own. But the main actors in "Greed" were only me and Miss Gish. I was sick, and the filming work was suspended and could not proceed. So Erich von Stroheim turned back halfway and had a big fight with me. He scolded me for being a bastard, having no conscience, being lazy, and making the whole team unable to work. In the end, he forced me to get up and go with him. Poor me, I had only rested for five days when I got up from the sickbed and set off with them. On the road, I stumbled and fell, my whole body was in pain, and I groaned constantly, but I had to endure the pain and move forward. My hatred for Erich von Stroheim at that time was indescribable.

In this way, our team moved forward slowly, passing through many places, even the names of which were strange and terrifying, until we reached a place called "Furnace Creek." This is the deepest part of Death Valley, much lower than sea level. There is a small village in Furnace Creek, which is the only place in the entire valley where traces of living people can be found. In this place, we settled down and filmed movies for two weeks, under the scorching sun. Further ahead, we reached "Devil's Golf Course," because this is the most rugged place in Death Valley. (To be continued)

Film Review

Review of "The Road" 229

— Ling He

I remember Mr. Zhang Shichuan once said in the first issue of "Star Monthly," "Please watch me go from 'Lipstick Market' to my 'Road,'" If we understand this sentence, then, we can see that he is quite confident in these two works. Of course, in "Lipstick Market," generally speaking, it can be considered above the standard, but what about "The Road"? It makes us unable to be satisfied.

Of course, in order to promote Chinese films to take a healthy path, we must engage in honest criticism.

Regarding the performance of The Road, the director's skills are indeed very lacking. Apart from the fact that the overall plot can progress in an orderly and uncomplicated manner, there are some aspects of the individual scenes that deserve our attention. The first is the portrayal of the protagonist, Su Lanying, which is truly unsatisfactory. After she became the wife of an official, her material life was naturally very rich, and her lifestyle would naturally change greatly. This can be proved by her love for puppies, but apart from raising puppies, she doesn't even understand the "fashion" of clothes, and even needs the instructions of a maid. When the tailor sent the new clothes, she was very feudal and hated his touching her hands and feet, but in another dance scene, she was actually willing to be hugged and danced and suddenly became "modern." Second, when Su Lanying, holding her sick husband, walked towards the luxurious hospital, the hospital nurses actually lined up to welcome her. From the tea boy to the accountant, they all bowed respectfully to this lady. Scenes like this are too "theatrical." Third, after Yao Junjie became an official, he actually "indulged" boldly in the office, which is also an exaggeration and inevitably untrue. Indeed, the intention is to expose the ugliness of the officialdom, but it is not so bad that it would be so bold even in the office. Fourth, when Su Lanying watched her husband and the social butterfly Pan Xuefen whispering sweet words, she actually stood there blankly for several minutes, while her husband acted as if she didn't exist, but at first she was flustered... There are many others, but unfortunately I can't remember them all at once. For example, that dance is not worth the effort. However, there are also many good things: such as seeing the shacks of the slums in the high-end hospital, and Pan Xuefen spying on Su Lanying's actions in the hotel, etc.

However, the content of a film is not limited to technical aspects, and whether the story is sound or not is the biggest key to the film.

Then, Mr. Ding Qianping, the screenwriter of "The Road," disappointed people after watching "Raging Current" and "Lipstick Market."

A famous woman will indeed often have extravagant hopes and will inevitably be raised by people with status in society. So Su Lanfen married a foreign student under the explanation of "a woman must have a lifelong commitment." Later, her husband became an official and changed his mind towards his wife. So Mr. Ding Qianping told us on the screen that this woman lost in love and did not hesitate to abandon her wife's status and still lived her actor's life. However, the subtitles say that she is unwilling to be insulted by men and strives for her personality and for her "future," but how does she strive? After the heroine did not receive her former lover, she shrugged her shoulders and gave a bitter smile, as if saying "Everything is over"! As for whether the wife of an official would be so brave and enlightened? It is also something we dare not imagine. However, the intention of the screenwriter lies in explaining the "women's occupation" issue, although in fact there is no way out, which is equivalent to no solution.

Regarding the performance, no actor achieved a high standard. Relatively speaking, Xuan Jinglin was still serious, and Zhu Qiuhen was also okay, but Wang Jiting was unpleasant.

However, the success of this film lies in the scenery and photography, where it can be seen that the skills of Chinese films are still improving.

Audience Comments

Review of "Flower of Hell" 230

— Zhu Ling

In a society under the capitalist system, love is completely built on money, banknotes, and cars. All social butterflies and beautiful girls will go into the arms of pot-bellied wealthy merchants and bankers, and poor boys will naturally not dare or be able to ask. This "Flower of Hell" writes about the typical American society where women generally use money as an exchange condition for love.

The story in the film can be said to be very complicated. The ending consciousness is contradictory. If the last paragraph is deleted, and it tells the story of a dissolute woman who exchanges her body for money, it could have become a powerful work exposing the deformed ugliness of capitalist society. However, the filmmakers were unwilling to do so and insisted on adding that incoherent story of a happy ending with a detective. As a result, it has only become a very ordinary pastime for the idle!

The acting skills are not bad. The director has a little cleverness. The opening close-up shots of several "scenery lines" in the restaurant are clever and concise. It is indeed not easy to perform such a complicated script so fluently and clearly. The editing of the scenes is appropriate, and small actions are given considerable consideration.

The heroine, May Vances, is appearing on the screen for the first time. Although she has not made any special contributions, it is gratifying that someone with very little screen experience can achieve such results. Her attitude is always very natural, and she expresses the mood of a dissolute woman who only wants money very thoroughly. Especially the charming attitude when singing, it is very much like Jean Harlow. The other supporting actors, Noah Beery, are mediocre, and Cary Grant is quite competent.

The pronunciation, photography, and lighting are as good as other Paramount films, and the taverns in the background are also very realistic and appropriate.

Joan Crawford Narrates a Strange Event 231

— Kang Bing

"Since I was a child, I have been afraid of the dark. Even though I know I am cowardly, no matter what, I am afraid of dark places. So my room is always lit with a small light from night to dawn," Joan Crawford said:

"Not long ago, I encountered a strange thing. At 11 o'clock one night, this light suddenly flickered as if it was about to go out. At that time, I didn't pay much attention, thinking it was just a problem with the current. Unexpectedly, at the same time the next night, from 11 o'clock to 12 o'clock, the light did the same again. So I called an electrician to repair the wire and the light. But no damage was found. On the third night, we all stayed in the house and guarded the light, turning on all the lights in the house. At 11 o'clock, the light in my room acted up again. On the fourth night, I moved my room to the living room, because I was afraid of the dark, and I installed another light outside. Unexpectedly, at 11 o'clock, the newly installed light flickered in the same way. We were all baffled."

"The next morning, I received a bad telegram from New York. It said that my closest friend had died last night. According to the telegram, she had been in the hospital for four days, and every night around 11 o'clock, she became very sad and missed me. After the fourth night, my light was just like usual. This is really an inexplicable thing."

An Eternal Regret: The Movie Novel The White Sister (Part 6) 232

— Si Ping

A Metro-Goldwyn-Mayer Production Starring Helen Hayes

Sacrificing Reputation and Happiness for Love

It really is strange, how life can change so abruptly. The colors are still the same, yet they are different; her heart feels a mysterious joy, a different kind of hope. He will surely come!—But in an instant, she is enveloped by the wings of doubt. He will surely not come!—Angela wrote a short note and sent it to the barracks. That dream is now naturally in the past. She hopes she hasn't made him too sad—he wouldn't really be worried about her, would he? Would he? She indulged in wishful thinking for a very long time.

"Goodbye, Vaudre," she whispered to herself. She stood with her eyes closed for a moment. Then, taking a deep breath, she walked out of the room.

Downstairs, in the grand living room, a dance was in progress to celebrate her engagement to Ernest. The music from the hidden orchestra floated up the curved staircase. At the foot of the staircase, her father was talking to Reverend Sarah Newnasser. Seeing her approaching, he smiled and proudly pulled her into his embrace, kissing her affectionately.

Angela fixed her gaze on his eyes. She wanted to confide in him her deepest feelings, but she was distressed and unable to speak. Feeling that she no longer had the courage, she turned to the pastor, asking him to take her to Ernest. As she was standing chatting with her fiancé, she suddenly heard a strangely familiar voice. Her heart pounding, she turned around and saw her father approaching with two men, a military officer in uniform and Giovani!

"My dear," Prince Sheremend said to Angela, "let me introduce you to Colonel Piff; this is my daughter, Angela." Angela, in a daze, said, "Good evening, Colonel."

"I am Lieutenant Severi," Giovani eagerly introduced himself.

"Good evening, Lieutenant," Angela said, struggling to breathe.

"This is my future son-in-law, Sir Trafalgar," the Prince continued the introductions. As everyone bowed respectfully, he added, "Do you remember this rascal, dear? He's the one who crashed into our car that day."

"Oh, yes, Father, I remember," Angela said, using all her strength to pretend it was a coincidence.

"Do you like to dance?" Giovani seized the opportunity to press his attack. Under the astonished gazes of those around them, he swept Angela into his arms and whirled her into the ballroom, where the melodious dance music drowned them out. Ernest, seeing this, asked angrily who that was. Piff immediately came to defuse the situation, saying he was a fearless aviator. Prince Sheremend suddenly realized, "So that's it! No wonder he came without an invitation." As the Prince spoke, he watched Angela and Giovani spin out of sight.
